code toronto star april 3 , 1993 from eliot improvements in automatic transmissions an excellent automatic can be found in the subaru legacy . </s> <s> it switches to sport mode when the electronics figure it , not when the driver sets the switch .. which is the proper way to do it , imo . </s> <s> so what does sport mode entail ? </s> <s> several things 1 revving to red line or to the rev limiter in the case of the legacy 2 delayed upshifts . </s> <s> I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> if you lift off briefly , it will remain in the low gear . </s> <s> this is handy if you are charging through corners and would like to do without the distraction of upshifts when there s another curve approaching 3 part throttle downshifts , based on the speed at which the pedal is depressed , rather than the position of the pedal . </s> <s> modern electronics can measure this very easily and switch to sport mode . </s> <s> this is wonderful if you want to charge through a green light about to turn red . </s> <s> my audi senses this very well and can downshift on as little as half throttle if my right foot is fast enough . </s> <s> also , I think that a smart automatic can deliver better gas mileage than a dumb driver with a stick , all else being equal .. remember that the idea of a stick being more economical than an automatic makes a big assumption that the driver is smart enough to know what gear to use for each situation .. how many times have you ridden with an inattentive driver cruising on the highway at 55 65 in 4th gear of a 5 speed ? </s> <s> how many of people who drive manuals really know what the best gear to use is for every conceivable situation ? </s> <s> I m sure there will be some who know , but I suspect that a chip controlled automatic with all possible scenario ratio combinations stored in rom is likely to do better . </s> <s> I can also say that all my previous assumptions were proved wrong after I got a car with instantaneous mpg readout ... high gear , low revs and wide open throttle is more economical than low gear , high revs and small throttle opening . </s> <s> the explanation is quite simple if one sits down to think about it , but not that obvious at first sight . </s> <s> eliotfrom matthew liggett opel owners ? </s> <s> in oriolefan uiuc writes craig boyle writes in article oriolefan uiuc writes darren gibbons writes I m looking for the most common one is probably the crank that is very similar to the i4 crank . </s> <s> which flat 4 engines have i4 style cranks ? </s> <s> comparing those two engines , the i4 and the flat 4 have no first order shaking forces or rocking moments . </s> <s> the i4 has a second order shaking force , while the flat 4 has a second order rocking moment . </s> <s> the significant thing about the flat 4 s second order moment is that it can be easily balanced out by adding mass at the ends of the crank . </s> <s> the i4 , however , requires a counter rotating shaft with mass to balance out the second order forces . </s> <s> I am 99.99 sure that subaru and porsche use the boxer configuration and not the inline 4 crank that you analyzed and compared . </s> <s> would you care to re evaluate the other case of a flat four ? </s> <s> I think that this configuration is perfectly balanced as far as primary , secondary forces and couples are concerned . </s> <s> I have an article in front of me that says so . </s> <s> bottom line the biggest difference between the engines would probably be their intended use . </s> <s> the flat 4 is easier to fit under low hoods and in rear compartments for mid or rear mounting . </s> <s> the i4 can be mounted transversely to reduce hood length read cab forward . </s> <s> other than that , there isn t much fanfare to the differences between them , no matter what subaru ads say . </s> <s> technology shared with porsche . </s> <s> indeed . </s> <s> the flat four is also shorter than an inline 4 , so even if it is mounted longitudinally it will not take up lots of length .. and a longitudinal placement is easier for a 4 wheel drive drivetrain . </s> <s> I think that subaru s ads hold water . </s> <s> in practice , their flat fours are noticeably smoother than inline 4s and completely buzz free , though some may not like its peculiar note . </s> <s> but as alfa has shown , a boxer four can produce a spine tingling scream that only the likes of </s> <s> energy secretary hails president s plan for alternative fuel vehicles to national desk , environment and energy reporters contact larry hart of the u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> department of energy , 202 586 5806 washington , april 21 secretary of energy hazel r . </s> <s> o leary today said president clinton s executive order on alternative fuels will make the federal government a driving force behind efforts to increase the availability of both alternative fuel vehicles and fuel supplies . </s> <s> president clinton signed the order today , which calls for federal purchases of alternative fuel vehicles in numbers over the next three years at least 50 percent higher than those called for in the energy policy act of 1992 . </s> <s> president clinton also announced that texas land commissioner gary mauro will head up the federal fleet conversion task force to advise o leary on implementation of the executive order . </s> <s> I am delighted that I will be working with gary mauro to make this happen , o leary said . </s> <s> as land commissioner , gary mauro has helped make texas a national leader in converting the state fleet to alternative fuels , and has been a tireless proponent of natural gas vehicles in speeches across the country . </s> <s> the task force is to issue a report within 90 days recommending a plan and schedule of implementation . </s> <s> the department of energy and all of us in government must lead by example if the option of alternative fuels is going to become a practical , affordable choice for fleet owners across the country , o leary said . </s> <s> increased use of domestically produced alternative fuels means reducing pollution while creating jobs . </s> <s> we believe that energy efficiency , protecting the environment , and a healthy economy are complimentary goals . </s> <s> o leary said that plans call for the department of energy to coordinate the agencies five year purchase plans , help with funding for extra purchase or conversion costs , and work with gsa to encourage development of the fuel infrastructure needed to make fleet conversions practical . </s> <s> under the order , the department of energy will also be working with states , local governments and industry to coordinate vehicle purchases and encourage manufacturers and fuel suppliers to make alternative fuel vehicles and alternative fuels .from john kennedy diatribe on us sold opels was opel owners ? </s> <s> darren gibbons writes I m looking for information on opel cars . </s> <s> now you ask , which model ? </s> <s> well , the sad truth is , I m not entirely sure , but it s a two seater , with roll over headlights , hard top , and really sporty looking . </s> <s> my friend has one sitting in his yard in really nice condition , body wise , but he transmission has seized up on him , so it hasn t run for a while . </s> <s> does anyone have any info on these cars ? </s> <s> the engine compartment looks really tight to work on , but it is in fine shape and I am quite interested in it . </s> <s> that would be the opel gt , sold in this country from 69 to 73 . </s> <s> it originally had a 1100 cc engine , which was later replaced by the 1900 cc . </s> <s> it was based on the old kadett drive train and suspension , with leaf springs in the rear and a single transverse leaf spring in the front . </s> <s> it looked good , but was limited as a performer . </s> <s> there has also been some discussion in this thread about the manta and other models . </s> <s> in 1971 opel introduced a new line of models , the 1900 series , that were also known as model numbers 51 , 57 , etc . </s> <s> these cars had the newer 1900cc engine and were available as two and four door coupes , a station wagon , and a sport coupe , known in europe as the manta . </s> <s> at the same time , there were two 30 series cars , which sold very few numbers , that also had the 1900 engine but the kadett suspension . </s> <s> the sport coupe , model 57 was also available as the rallye , 57r , with a blacked out hood , tach , and fog lights , but was mechanically the same except for a numerically higher rear end ratio . </s> <s> in 1973 the sport coupe was also named the manta in the us . </s> <s> 1973 was the last year for the gt in any country , both because of the us bumper height regulations and the fact that fiat exercised an option on the factory that opel was leasing to build the gts . </s> <s> the 1900 series continued in 1974 with minor body differences . </s> <s> in 1975 , the manta , 1900 sedan also called the ascona and the wagon were available with bosch electronic fuel injection . </s> <s> these cars also had larger brakes and wider wheels . </s> <s> these cars were starting to compete with the 1975 buick century low price leader of the time , and were the last opels imported into the us . </s> <s> from 1976 to 1979 , cars that sported buick opel badges were still sold by the buick dealers , but were rebadged isuzu I marks . </s> <s> the idea was to call them opels instead of changing the dealers neon signs . </s> <s> various models of the 50 series cars dominated the showroom stock racing of the 70 s in their class , and were known as serious 2002 competition . </s> <s> parts are still available from a number of sources . </s> <s> I still have a 73 manta and two 75 sedans and all the on what kind of locking lugnuts you have . </s> <s> my previous car had locking lugnuts that weighed about 2.5 oz . </s> <s> more than the others . </s> <s> the locking lugnuts were factory equipment , and according to the factory service manual , after tire balancing the technician mechanic was supposed to put a 1 2 oz . </s> <s> counterweight on the rim opposite the locking nut . </s> <s> I always had vibration problems with those stupid lugnuts since no one ever did the service correctly . </s> <s> I eventually got rid of the locking lugnuts and replaced them with the standard lugnuts . </s> <s> unfortunately , I found out about the counterweighting technique 6 months after I got rid of the locking nuts . </s> <s> my present car , a saturn sc , has locking lugnuts that I bought at the dealer and are made specifically for the saturn . </s> <s> they have been made to be exactly the same weight as the non locking lugnuts said so on the package and I verified it myself . </s> <s> I haven t had any vibration problems with the tires at all due to the nuts in 12,000 of ownership . </s> <s> I did have some other vibration problems , but it was due to a poor job of tire balancing . diesels are turbocharged . </s> <s> 2 . </s> <s> all use an aftercooler , which cools the air which was heated by compression by the turbocharger up to about 25 psi . </s> <s> 3 . </s> <s> a gismo on the injector pump which senses the pressurized air intake , and limits full delivery of fuel while the pressure is low . </s> <s> no scrubbers , catalytic converters , etc , are used . </s> <s> the path from the turbocharger to the exhaust outlet is kept very free . </s> <s> interestingly , except for the low pressure fuel limitation , power output and mileage are enhanced by these measures . university of toronto , eecg , computer graphics do not weave between traffic cones at road works . </s>  <s> from the new british highway code toronto star april 3 , 1993 </s>  <s> from eliot subject re improvements in automatic transmissions an excellent automatic can be found in the subaru legacy . </s>  <s> it switches to sport mode when the electronics figure it , not when the driver sets the switch .. which is the proper way to do it , imo . </s>  <s> so what does sport mode entail ? </s>  <s> several things 1 revving to red line or to the rev limiter in the case of the legacy 2 delayed upshifts . </s>  <s> I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> if you lift off briefly , it will remain in the low gear . </s>  <s> this is handy if you are charging through corners and would like to do without the distraction of upshifts when there s another curve approaching 3 part throttle downshifts , based on the speed at which the pedal is depressed , rather than the position of the pedal . </s>  <s> modern electronics can measure this very easily and switch to sport mode . </s>  <s> this is wonderful if you want to charge through a green light about to turn red . </s>  <s> my audi senses this very well and can downshift on as little as half throttle if my right foot is fast enough . </s>  <s> also , I think that a smart automatic can deliver better gas mileage than a dumb driver with a stick , all else being equal .. remember that the idea of a stick being more economical than an automatic makes a big assumption that the driver is smart enough to know what gear to use for each situation .. how many times have you ridden with an inattentive driver cruising on the highway at 55 65 in 4th gear of a 5 speed ? </s>  <s> how many of people who drive manuals really know what the best gear to use is for every conceivable situation ? </s>  <s> I m sure there will be some who know , but I suspect that a chip controlled automatic with all possible scenario ratio combinations stored in rom is likely to do better . </s>  <s> I can also say that all my previous assumptions were proved wrong after I got a car with instantaneous mpg readout ... high gear , low revs and wide open throttle is more economical than low gear , high revs and small throttle opening . </s>  <s> the explanation is quite simple if one sits down to think about it , but not that obvious at first v4 v6 v8 v12 vx ? </s>  <s> in article brian j queiser writes there are two crank configurations for the flat 4 the most common one is probably the crank that is very similar to the i4 crank . </s>  <s> which flat 4 engines have i4 style cranks ? </s>  <s> comparing those two engines , the i4 and the flat 4 have no first order shaking forces or rocking moments . </s>  <s> the i4 has a second order shaking force , while the flat 4 has a second order rocking moment . </s>  <s> the significant thing about the flat 4 s second order moment is that it can be easily balanced out by adding mass at the ends of the crank . </s>  <s> the i4 , however , requires a counter rotating shaft with mass to balance out the second order forces . </s>  <s> I am 99.99 sure that subaru and porsche use the boxer configuration and not the inline 4 crank that you analyzed and compared . </s>  <s> would you care to re evaluate the other case of a flat four ? </s>  <s> I think that this configuration is perfectly balanced as far as primary , secondary forces and couples are concerned . </s>  <s> I have an article in front of me that says so . </s>  <s> bottom line the biggest difference between the engines would probably be their intended use . </s>  <s> the flat 4 is easier to fit under low hoods and in rear compartments for mid or rear mounting . </s>  <s> the i4 can be mounted transversely to reduce hood length read cab forward . </s>  <s> other than that , there isn t much fanfare to the differences between them , no matter what subaru ads say . </s>  <s> technology shared with porsche . </s>  <s> indeed . </s>  <s> the flat four is also shorter than an inline 4 , so even if it is mounted longitudinally it will not take up lots of length .. and a longitudinal placement is easier for a 4 wheel drive drivetrain . </s>  <s> I think that subaru s ads hold water . </s>  <s> in practice , their flat fours are noticeably smoother than inline 4s and completely buzz free , though some may not like its peculiar note . </s>  <s> but as alfa has shown , a boxer four can produce a spine tingling scream that only the likes of recent hondas can approach . </s>  <s> eliot </s>  <s> from erini honda civic si civic coupes del sol si nissan nx1600 nx2000 mazda mx 3 isuzu impulse geo storm ford escort gt if you look at the prices of these cars , they re more expensive than they re 4 door counterparts . </s>  <s> the is good reason for this . </s>  <s> it is a more upscale and trend driven market . </s>  <s> even though many of these models are based on sedan platforms , their interior , etc . </s>  <s> is good enough to warrant slightly higher prices . </s>  <s> here are some of the platform derivations I can think of tercel paseo sentra nx1600 nx2000 civic del sol 323 mx 3 not sure on this one stylus impulse storm to illustrate , a tercel starts at around 8000 , while the paseo starts at around 11,000 . </s>  <s> even a 4 door tercel will cost less than a 2 door paseo . </s>  <s> now , you might be saying that the tercel doesn t offer the power that some 4 doors offer . </s>  <s> what I mean is that there is no 4 dr tercel with a comparable powerplant as its sport coupe derivative . </s>  <s> let s take another example the isuzu stylus xs and impulse xs storm gsi . </s>  <s> both have the same powerplants a 1.6 l 140hp engine , but the smaller 2 dr coupes are generally more expensive . </s>  <s> again , this is because the two door sport coupe market is a more fashion oriented and trend setting segment . </s>  <s> people are willing to pay more money for this type of car . </s>  <s> in short , even though the sc1 sc2 may be smaller , hence less car , it s market orientation dictates a slightly higher price than its mechanically equivalent sedan sl1 sl2 version . </s>  <s> I hope this clears things up a bit ... mihir shah </s>  <s> from thunderbirds are go ! </s>  <s> ! </s>  <s> ! </s>  <s> subject mr2 noisy engine . </s>  <s> g day people , are president s plan for alternative fuel vehicles to national desk , environment and energy reporters contact larry hart of the u . </s>  <s> s . </s>  <s> department of energy , 202 586 5806 washington , april 21 secretary of energy hazel r . </s>  <s> o leary today said president clinton s executive order on alternative fuels will make the federal government a driving force behind efforts to increase the availability of both alternative fuel vehicles and fuel supplies . </s>  <s> president clinton signed the order today , which calls for federal purchases of alternative fuel vehicles in numbers over the next three years at least 50 percent higher than those called for in the energy policy act of 1992 . </s>  <s> president clinton also announced that texas land commissioner gary mauro will head up the federal fleet conversion task force to advise o leary on implementation of the executive order . </s>  <s> I am delighted that I will be working with gary mauro to make this happen , o leary said . </s>  <s> as land commissioner , gary mauro has helped make texas a national leader in converting the state fleet to alternative fuels , and has been a tireless proponent of natural gas vehicles in speeches across the country . </s>  <s> the task force is to issue a report within 90 days recommending a plan and schedule of implementation . </s>  <s> the department of energy and all of us in government must lead by example if the option of alternative fuels is going to become a practical , affordable choice for fleet owners across the country , o leary said . </s>  <s> increased use of domestically produced alternative fuels means reducing pollution while creating jobs . </s>  <s> we believe that energy efficiency , protecting the environment , and a healthy economy are complimentary goals . </s>  <s> o leary said that plans call for the department of energy to coordinate the agencies five year purchase plans , help with funding for extra purchase or conversion costs , and work with gsa to encourage development of the fuel infrastructure needed to make fleet conversions practical . </s>  <s> under the order , the department of energy will also be working with states , local governments and industry to coordinate vehicle purchases and encourage manufacturers and fuel suppliers to make alternative fuel vehicles and alternative fuels more widely available . about a year ago I found that the master cylinder on the clutch in the 84 was leaking fluid around the piston seal , leading to air in the system and fluid back into the passenger compartment of the car . </s>  <s> I pulled the plunger and got a rebuild kit new plunger , seal , etc . </s>  <s> and thought I had the problem licked . </s>  <s> much to my surprise , the same problem developed . </s>  <s> ever since I have been periodically feeding the clutch hydraulins additional fluid and bleeding air from the system . </s>  <s> I knew I would be selling the car and didn t want to go all the way to solving the problem . </s>  <s> I should add that the clutch is original , and that I ve had to adjust the pedal to allow maximum extension of the piston into the master cylinder in order to actuate the clutch . </s>  <s> my hypothesis is that this means that when fully depressing the clutch pedal , the angle of the piston rod attached to the pedal is off the axix of the cylinder , assist , so only legs had enough strength to activate them . </s>  <s> since then , it s been traditional and people would have a hard time getting used to anything else . </s>  <s> well , where , exactly , would you put a hand clutch and brake ? </s>  <s> on a motorcycle , it s easy the handlebars have a very limited range of turning . </s>  <s> steering wheels , on the other hand , turn around and around and around ... which is fine for electrical relays like your cruise control and airbag but how many of you want to lose your clutch and or brake due to a short circuit ? </s>  <s> shades of the edsel ! </s>  <s> they had pushbuttons in the steering wheel hub that controlled the auto tranny . </s>  <s> it was very disconcerting to shift into reverse when turning a corner and the wires shorted . </s>  <s> there are workarounds , but there s really no reason to use hand power on a car s clutch or brakes , and lightening them to the point that they are finesse controls suitable for hand use would increse the mechanical complexity substantially look at power brakes and non power brakes for an example . </s>  <s> I saw an experimental car that had a joystick instead of a steering wheel ... that s about useless , imho . </s>  <s> another automotive oddity is separate keys for trunks , doors , and ignitions . </s>  <s> why on earth would you want this ? </s>  <s> I know I don t . </s>  <s> I want a separate trunk key for security reasons it gives me a totally separate , lockable container . </s>  <s> for door and ignition ... ehhh , the same key s ok , I guess . </s> cattle trails and in wagon ruts . </s>  <s> I am fairly sure that placement of the steering wheel was pretty much arbitrary to the company at that time ... by the 1920s , there was a very active good roads movement , which had its origins actually in the 1890s during the bicycle craze , picked up steam in the teens witness the linclon highway association , 1912 or so , and the us highway support act real name something different in 1916 that first pledged federal aid to states and counties to build decent roads . </s>  <s> also , the experience of widespread use of trucks for domestic transport during ww 1 convinced the government that good raods were crucial to our national defense . </s>  <s> anyway , by the 20s there were plenty of good roads , at least around urban areas , and with anything except your elbow . </s>  <s> if you have pieces of ring , con rods , valve heads or stems , just reach into the sump through the hole in the block that was associated with the creation of those large bits and pieces . </s>  <s> anything you can t remove with one hand through the hole in the block may safely be left in place . </s>  <s> from john kennedy subject diatribe on us sold opels was re opel owners ? </s>  <s> darren gibbons writes I m looking for information on opel cars . </s>  <s> now you ask , which model ? </s>  <s> well , the sad truth is , I m not entirely sure , but it s a two seater , with roll over headlights , hard top , and really sporty looking . </s>  <s> my friend has one sitting in his yard in really nice condition , body wise , but he transmission has seized up on him , so it hasn t run for a while . </s>  <s> does anyone have any info on these cars ? </s>  <s> the engine compartment looks really tight to work on , but it is in fine shape and I am quite interested in it . </s>  <s> that would be the opel gt , sold in this country from 69 to 73 . </s>  <s> it originally had a 1100 cc engine , which was later replaced by the 1900 cc . </s>  <s> it was based on the old kadett drive train and suspension , with leaf springs in the rear and a single transverse leaf spring in the front . </s>  <s> it looked good , but was limited as a performer . </s>  <s> there has also been some discussion in this thread about the manta and other models . </s>  <s> in 1971 opel introduced a new line of models , the 1900 series , that were also known as model numbers 51 , 57 , etc . </s>  <s> these cars had the newer 1900cc engine and were available as two and four door coupes , a station wagon , and a sport coupe , known in europe as the manta . </s>  <s> at the same time , there were two 30 series cars , which sold very few numbers , that also had the 1900 engine but the kadett suspension . </s>  <s> the sport coupe , model 57 was also available as the rallye , 57r , with a blacked out hood , tach , and fog lights , but was mechanically the same except for a numerically higher rear end ratio . </s>  <s> in 1973 the sport coupe was also named the manta in the us . </s>  <s> 1973 was the last year for the gt in any country , both because of the us bumper height regulations and the fact that fiat exercised an option on the factory that opel was leasing to build the gts . </s>  <s> the 1900 series continued in 1974 with minor body differences . </s>  <s> in 1975 , the manta , 1900 sedan also called the ascona and the wagon were available with bosch electronic fuel injection . </s>  <s> these cars also had larger brakes and wider wheels . </s>  <s> these cars were starting to compete with the 1975 buick century low price leader of the time , and were the last opels imported into the us . </s>  <s> from 1976 to 1979 , cars that sported buick opel badges were still sold by the buick dealers , but were rebadged isuzu I marks . </s>  <s> the idea was to call them opels instead of changing the dealers neon signs . </s>  <s> various models of the 50 series cars dominated the showroom stock racing of the 70 s in their class , and were known as serious 2002 competition . </s>  <s> parts are still available from a number of sources . </s>  <s> I still have a 73 manta and two 75 sedans and all the trick parts I could collect in 20 years . </s>  <s> john kennedy uunet ! </s>  <s> opel ! </s>  <s> johnk second source , inc . </s>  <s> annapolis , md </s>  <s> from jerry bowman subject re v4 v6 v8 v12 vx ? </s> locking lugnut on your tires , do you need to have your tires rebalanced ? </s>  <s> ? </s>  <s> john mas e mail address well , it depends on what kind of locking lugnuts you have . </s>  <s> my previous car had locking lugnuts that weighed about 2.5 oz . </s>  <s> more than the others . </s>  <s> the locking lugnuts were factory equipment , and according to the factory service manual , after tire balancing the technician mechanic was supposed to put a 1 2 oz . </s>  <s> counterweight on the rim opposite the locking nut . </s>  <s> I always had vibration problems with those stupid lugnuts since no one ever did the service correctly . </s>  <s> I eventually got rid of the locking lugnuts and replaced them with the standard lugnuts . </s>  <s> unfortunately , I found out about the counterweighting technique 6 months after I got rid of the locking nuts . </s>  <s> my present car , a saturn sc , has locking lugnuts that I bought at the dealer and are made specifically for the saturn . </s>  <s> they have been made to be exactly the same weight as the non locking lugnuts said so on the package and I verified it myself . </s>  <s> I haven t had any vibration problems with the tires at all due to the nuts in 12,000 of ownership . </s>  <s> I did have some other vibration problems , but it was due to a poor job of tire balancing . </s>  <s> tom </s>  <s> from kris a .
